\DoxyCodeLine{01700\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ensure\ that\ the\ string\ remains\ valid\ as\ long\ as\ it\ might\ be\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01701\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ use\ an\ std::map\ to\ do\ so.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01703\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01704\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Because\ putenv\ stores\ a\ pointer\ to\ the\ string\ buffer,\ we\ can't\ delete\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01705\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ previous\ string\ (if\ present)\ until\ after\ it's\ replaced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01706\ \ \ std::string*\ prev\_env\ =\ NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01707\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (added\_env.find(name)\ !=\ added\_env.end())\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{01709\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01710\ \ \ added\_env[name]\ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{01711\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{new}\ std::string((\mbox{\hyperlink{classtesting_1_1_message}{Message}}()\ <<\ name\ <<\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}="{}}\ <<\ value).GetString());}
\DoxyCodeLine{01712\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01713\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ standard\ signature\ of\ putenv\ accepts\ a\ 'char*'\ argument.\ Other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01714\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ implementations,\ like\ C++Builder's,\ accept\ a\ 'const\ char*'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01715\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ cast\ away\ the\ 'const'\ since\ that\ would\ work\ for\ both\ variants.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01716\ \ \ putenv(\textcolor{keyword}{const\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*\textcolor{keyword}{>}(added\_env[name]-\/>c\_str()));}
\DoxyCodeLine{01717\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{delete}\ prev\_env;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01718\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif\ defined(GTEST\_OS\_WINDOWS)\ \ }\textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ we\ are\ on\ Windows\ proper.}}
